(runtime.Object, error) {\n    // ... validation and preparation ...\n    key, err := e.KeyFunc(ctx, name)\n    ttl, err := e.calculateTTL(obj, 0, false)\n    out := e.NewFunc()\n    if err := e.Storage.Create(ctx, key, obj, out, ttl, ...); err != nil {\n        // ... error handling ...\n    }\n    return out, nil\n}\n```\n\n### 2. **etcd3 Storage Backend** (Kubernetes Adapter Layer)\n**File:** `/workspace/kubernetes/staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/storage/etcd3/store.go:241`\n\nThe `Store.Create()` method in etcd3 storage encodes the object and sends it to etcd:\n```go\nfunc (s *store) Create(ctx context.Context, key string, obj, out runtime.Object, ttl uint64) error {\n    preparedKey, err := s.prepareKey(key)\n    // Encode the object to bytes\n    data, err := runtime.Encode(s.codec, obj)\n    \n    // Transform data for encryption/compression if needed\n    newData, err := s.transformer.TransformToStorage(ctx, data, ...)\n    \n    // Call OptimisticPut on the etcd client\n    txnResp, err := s.client.Kubernetes.OptimisticPut(ctx, preparedKey, newData, 0, kubernetes.PutOptions{LeaseID: lease})\n    \n    // Return the response\n    return nil\n}\n```\n\n### 3. **etcd Client - Transaction Builder** (etcd Client Layer)\n**File:** `/workspace/etcd/client/v3/kubernetes/client.go:83`\n\nThe client builds and commits a conditional transaction:\n```go\nfunc (k Client) OptimisticPut(ctx context.Context, key string, value []byte, expectedRevision int64, opts PutOptions) (resp PutResponse, err error) {\n    txn := k.KV.Txn(ctx).If(\n        clientv3.Compare(clientv3.ModRevision(key), \"=\", expectedRevision),\n    ).Then(\n        clientv3.OpPut(key, string(value), clientv3.WithLease(opts.LeaseID)),\n    )\n    \n    txnResp, err := txn.Commit()  // Sends to etcd server\n    return resp, nil\n}\n```\n\n### 4. **etcd Server RPC Handler** (etcd Server gRPC Layer)\n**File:** `/workspace/etcd/server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/key.go:55`\n\nThe gRPC server receives the Put request:\n```go\nfunc (s *kvServer) Put(ctx context.Context, r *pb.PutRequest) (*pb.PutResponse, error) {\n    if err := checkPutRequest(r); err != nil {\n        return nil, err\n    }\n    resp, err := s.kv.Put(ctx, r)  // s.kv is EtcdServer\n    s.hdr.fill(resp.Header)\n    return resp, nil\n}\n```\n\n### 5. **etcd Server - RAFT Replication** (etcd Server RAFT Layer)\n**File:** `/workspace/etcd/server/etcdserver/v3_server.go:139`\n\nThe Put request is wrapped in a RAFT log entry and replicated:\n```go\nfunc (s *EtcdServer) Put(ctx context.Context, r *pb.PutRequest) (*pb.PutResponse, error) {\n    ctx = context.WithValue(ctx, traceutil.StartTimeKey, time.Now())\n    resp, err := s.raftRequest(ctx, pb.InternalRaftRequest{Put: r})\n    return resp.(*pb.PutResponse), nil\n}\n```\n\nThe `raftRequest()` method sends the request through RAFT consensus, ensuring the request is committed and replicated across the cluster.\n\n### 6. **Apply Committed RAFT Entries** (etcd Server Apply Layer)\n**File:** `/workspace/etcd/server/etcdserver/apply.go:169-171`\n\nOnce the RAFT entry is committed, it's applied to the state machine:\n```go\ncase r.Put != nil:\n    op = \"Put\"\n    ar.resp, ar.trace, ar.err = a.s.applyV3.Put(context.TODO(), nil, r.Put)\n```\n\n### 7. **Apply Put to MVCC Store** (MVCC Layer)\n**File:** `/workspace/etcd/server/etcdserver/apply.go:249-302`\n\nThe put is applied to the MVCC transaction:\n```go\nfunc (a *applierV3backend) Put(ctx context.Context, txn mvcc.TxnWrite, p *pb.PutRequest) (...) {\n    resp := &pb.PutResponse{}\n    val, leaseID := p.Value, lease.LeaseID(p.Lease)\n    \n    if txn == nil {\n        txn = a.s.KV().Write(trace)  // Create a write transaction\n        defer txn.End()\n    }\n    \n    // Put the key-value pair into the MVCC transaction\n    resp.Header.Revision = txn.Put(p.Key, val, leaseID)\n    return resp, trace, nil\n}\n```\n\n### 8. **MVCC Transaction -
